【Sales Amount for Out of Stocks and Shrinkage Not Updated】
问题: Sales Amount for Out of Stocks and Shrinkage Not Updated

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Type: Incident
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue:
Dashboard Sales Amount for Out of Stocks and Shrinkage Breakdown is not updated vs store sales.

Dashboard Sales Amount (Jan 1-31, 2026)
Out of Stocks Report - 60.5M
Shrinkage

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:Sales Amount for Out of Stocks and Shrinkage Not Updated

Root Cause Analysis: User Knowledge

Resolution:
- Requester is confuse as to whyDashboard Sales Amount for Out of Stocks and Shrinkage Breakdown is not updated vs store sales.
- After checking with DMall R&D, they have confirmed that on Out of Sock and Shrinkage Breakdown belong to Inventory Manage reports which only count those item/article that has inventory. And those item that are not managed in inventory will not be counted.Store Performance Analysis is a sales report, which will include all sales data. The data differences are due to the business differences of the reports themselves
- Inform the requester.
- No further asisstance needed. Closing as resolved



Release Notes/Version:

Remarks/Recommendation:

Data Collection/References:

【Nakapag pre-com na tas nakapag log inn at na pick up-an pa】
问题: Nakapag pre-com na tas nakapag log inn at na pick up-an pa

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type:Nakapag pre-com na tas nakapag log inn at na pick up-an paResponse Level:Called IT H.O tas for manage engine daw po ang response sa akin.
Details of Issue: Instead of pick up, pre commit po ang nagawa ni Cashier na hindi po alam ng r

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:Inquiry on Double Cashier Float settlement

Root Cause Analysis:User Procedural Problem
Upon verification in DMall, two (2) cashier float/loan transactions were recorded.
As confirmed by Sir Adrian, the cashier mistakenly performed a pre-commit transaction instead of a pickup. As a result, no pickup slip was generated. The cashier subsequently logged in again, triggering another automatic float amounting to PHP 3,000, which is expected system behavior.
Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and called the store.
2.As confirmed by Sir Adrian, the cashier mistakenly performed a pre-commit transaction instead of a pickup. As a result, no pickup slip was generated. The cashier subsequently logged in again, triggering another automatic float amounting to PHP 3,000, which is expected system behavior.
3. Sir Adrian also requested guidance on any additional actions required in this incident, aside from preparing a cashier adjustment report, as this may potentially impact sales records and accounting reconciliation.
4. Loop in SM POS team, Accounting and Operations for reference.
5.Resolved the ticket.

Remarks/Recommendation:-

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - EOD Failure

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

SVI STTB(5035)
-Upon checking with successful EOD but NO EOD files created.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:NO EOD FILES
Root Cause Analysis: Defect from DMall

Resolution:There is a post-sales order that requires the system to reference the original (positive) order during the reconciliation process. However, the original order was already removed from the 0006 database one month ago. As a result, the upstream and downstream reconciliation process failed, and the EOD file was not generated.
After-sales order number:9557701006260201152325002
Original order date:February 1, 2026


The original positive transaction corresponds to receipt number557701025251221194331400314, with an order date ofDecember 21, 2025.



Root cause: Recently, we manually deleted the data in the intermediate library biz_osi_sales_order from POS orders to big data, retaining only 1 months' worth upon SM approvalWhen this order was undergoing reconciliation verification, the positive order was queried through the after-sales order. Since the positive order was from December, it could not be found, resulting in a blockage in the reconciliation process. 

Temporary Solution:
Restore this after-sales order from the big data database, and then the task will automatically retry to generate EOD. 

Long-term solution:
Change the query steps of the Finance service to query from the POS order database.

Included in Problem Management under Problem #: 318.

Ticket resolved

【NO AUTOMATIC FLOAT WAS GENERATED FOR ALL OPENING CASHIERS】
问题: NO AUTOMATIC FLOAT WAS GENERATED FOR ALL OPENING CASHIERS

根因分类: Network / Connectivity Failure

具体根因: Network - POS / ISP Connection Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request:NO AUTOMATIC FLOAT WAS GENERATED FOR ALL OPENING CASHIERSResponse Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:
During the cashier's sign in on the pos system, the automatic float was not generated for all opening c

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:Opening cashier POS have no automatic loan upon login

Root Cause Analysis:ISP downtime
POS can't connect to the ISP during cashier login

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2.Based on the logs, the ISP experienced downtime from 9:24 AM to 11:56 AM on February 3, 2026. During this period, all POS terminals were unable to connect to the ISP at the time of cashier login. As a result, there were no automatic float/loan.3. Informed the store that this is a normal system behavior under such scenario.
4. Also advised them to ensure that the POS terminals have a stable network connection during operation and that the ISP is up and running.
5. Resolved the ticket.

Remarks/Recommendation:-

【NO EOD FILES】
问题: NO EOD FILES

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: SVI CALOOCAN (5719)
-Perform manual reconciliation but still no EOD files generated

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SVI Caloocan TD: 2/5/2026

Root Cause Analysis:A return transaction(After-Sales Receipt No. 9558916015260205163637001)was processed on February 5, 2026 at 4:36 PM.
The transaction containsArticle 20168848, which has already been delisted in SAP and synchronized to DMall.
SinceArticle 20168848no longer exists in Store 5719, the EOD file generation verification logic is unable to locate the item during validation. As a result, the system fails to generate the EOD files.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chanda and SM teamthat this is the same issue previously encountered in SMCo La Trinidad(Ticket No. 6489369)and has already been logged under Problem No. 321.
3. Askedfor SM assistance and approval to proceed with the necessary corrective actions.4. Informed them thatDMall recommends to temporarily list/restore the article 20168848 in SVI Caloocan and wait for the EOD files to generate automatically before delisting it again.
5. Masterdata confirmed that the article was already relisted. Informed them that the EOD files were already generated.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

Image 2. Article 20168848 status in Store Article Mgt



Image 3. Generated EOD files

【NO DATA FOUND  AT IN-STORE  POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT】
问题: NO DATA FOUND  AT IN-STORE  POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Data Source Issue

问题描述: BRANCH: SVI MASINAG, SVI MAKATI,SVI NOVALICHES, SVI ROSARIO,SVI BACOLOD

          NO DATA FOUND AT IN-STORE POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT  DATED:02-08-2026.&nb

解决摘要: Log to Problem

解决方案:
Define Issue:No data found at In-Store POS Server Reconciliation Mgt Page (SVI Masinag, Makati, Novaliches, Rosario and Bacolod)TD: 2/8/2026

Root Cause Analysis:
During the daily EOD reconciliation, each POS terminal validates SI (Sales Invoice) continuity.
For these stores, some of the POS terminal had no transactions for a long period—the last transaction was about approximately one and a half months ago.
However, the POS MySQL database only retains one month of data due to archiving, so the previous SI could not be found.
When the SI cannot be found, the reconciliation process records all missing SI entries, resulting in an excessively large data set and causing an error when saving to the database.
As a result, the system fails to generate the EOD files.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed SMthat no EOD files were generated for SVI Masinag, Makati, Novaliches, Rosario and BacolodTD: 2/8/2026. The root cause analysis, temporary and long-term solutions were also provided.3. Asked Maam Chanda's approval to proceed with the necessary corrective actions.
4.DMall R&D manually add a reconciliation record with the status set toFailed.
5. AdvisedSM POS team to click the"ManualSuccess"in the Reconciliation page to generate theEOD files.
6. Informed SM that the EOD files were already generated.
7. Sent thelist of POS terminals across all tenants that have not been used for at least one (1) month andadvised SM totemporarily refrain from using those POS (during Chinese New Year)to minimize potential EOD and reconciliation-related issues
8. Added this ticket to Problem 322.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:
Image 1. SVI Bacolod Inbound


Image 2. SVI Rosario Inbound



Image 3. SVI Novaliches Inbound



Image 4. SVI Makati Inbound



Image 5. SVI Masinag Inbound

Define Issue:No data found at In-Store POS Server Reconciliation Mgt Page (SSM Bicutan and SSM Valenzuela)TD: 2/8/2026

Root Cause Analysis:
During the daily EOD reconciliation, each POS terminal validates SI (Sales Invoice) continuity.
For these stores, some of the POS terminal had no transactions for a long period—the last transaction was about approximately one and a half months ago.
However, the POS MySQL database only retains one month of data due to archiving, so the previous SI could not be found. 
When the SI cannot be found, the reconciliation process records all missing SI entries, resulting in an excessively large data set and causing an error when saving to the database.
As a result, the system fails to generate the EOD files.
Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed SMthat no EOD files were generated for SSM Bicutan and Valenzuela TD: 2/8/2026. The root cause analysis, temporary and long-term solutions were also provided.

7. Sent thelist of POS terminals across all tenants that have not been used for at least one (1) month andadvised SM totemporarily refrain from using those POS (during Chinese New Year)to minimize potential EOD and reconciliation-related issues

AD ID: *

Affected Markets User:
SVI - SUPERVALUE, INC.
Company: *
SVI / Supervalue, Inc.
Branch

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:No eSales file generated for Roving POS Machines (January 2026)

Root Cause Analysis:User Knowledge
Current system behavior is thateSales files are generated only when there are transactions recorded in the POS/store
No transactions → no reconciliation → no EOD files including the eSales file

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed Maam Chantal thatthe current behavior of the DMall system is thateSales files are generated only when there are transactions recorded in the POS/store. 
3. No transactions → no reconciliation → no EOD files including the eSales file.Manual generation of eSales files is also not supported by the system.
4. As per SM IT, no Roving POS devices were used in January 2026, and therefore, no transactions exist for that period.Resolved the ticket.

【DMall Apps Concern: POS Sales - SRP of certain articles not correct】
问题: DMall Apps Concern: POS Sales - SRP of certain articles not correct

根因分类: Defect from SM

具体根因: Hardware - Weighing Scale Install, Setup and Configuration

问题描述: New Ticket Creation Template
Contact Person: *
Melody O. Co
Contact Number / MS Teams: *
09178151917
Email Address: *
mo.co@smmarkets.com.ph
AD ID: *

Affected Markets User:
Supervalue, Inc. (SM Supermarket)
Company: *
Supervalue,

解决摘要: --

解决方案:
Define Issue:POS Sales - SRP of certain articles not correct
Root Cause Analysis:The barcode generated by one of the weighing scales in SVI Legazpi is incorrectly configured.
Configuration is set toSI base unit (kilograms)instead of grams.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.DMall R&D team confirmed that thearticle price data sent via SFTP (CSV file) was correct.3. SM IT provided asample sticker label and found some discrepancy or inconsistency in terms of weight unit.The label indicatesPRICE/KG, however, theweight is printed in grams, resulting in a unit mismatch
4. Based on the 20-digit barcode printed by the weighing scale, the weight was 12kg which should only be 1.2kg.
5. Informed SM team that the the DMall POS system logic is consistent as designed and aligns with the approved blueprint.
6.Advised them to update the weighing scale configuration to useSI base unit (kilograms)instead of grams to prevent incorrect unit price computation.
7. Resolved the ticket.

【NO DATA FOUND AT IN-STORE POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT】
问题: NO DATA FOUND AT IN-STORE POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Data Source Issue

问题描述: BRANCH: SSM PULILAN
DATE: 02-13-2026

NO DATA FOUND AT IN-STORE POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT DATED:02-13-2026

解决摘要: Data Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:NO DATA FOUND AT IN-STORE POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT(SSM Pulilan TD: 02/13/2026)
Root Cause Analysis:The data was archived, there were too many missing SIs, which caused an error when writing to the database. This affected the execution of creating reconciliation records for the next store.As a result, the system fails to generate the EOD files.
Resolution:
-Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
-Informed SMthat no EOD files were generated for SSM Pulilan TD: 02/13/2026. The root cause analysis, temporary and long-term solutions were also provided.
-According to our R&D,issue occurred during the 5:00 PM scheduled task that supplements and generates reconciliation records. The previous store encountered an error because the missing SI field exceeded the allowed length due to data archiving, which caused the process to fail and affected the generation of reconciliation records for the subsequent store.
-DMall R&D manually add a reconciliation record with the status set toFailed.
-AdvisedSM POS team to click the"ManualSuccess"in the Reconciliation page to generate theEOD files.
-Informed SM that the EOD files were already generated.
-Added this ticket to Problem 322.Resolved the ticket.
Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

【NO DATA FOUND  AT IN-STORE  POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT】
问题: NO DATA FOUND  AT IN-STORE  POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Data Source Issue

问题描述: BRANCH: SVI BAGUIO
 NO DATA FOUND AT IN-STORE POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT DATED:02-13-2026.

解决摘要: Log to Problem

解决方案:
Define Issue:NO DATA FOUND AT IN-STORE POS SERVER RECONCILIATION MGT (SVI Baguio TD: 02/13/2026)

Root Cause Analysis:
During the daily EOD reconciliation, each POS terminal validates SI (Sales Invoice) continuity.
For these stores, some of the POS terminal had no transactions for a long period—the last transaction was about approximately one and a half months ago.
However, the POS MySQL database only retains one month of data due to archiving, so the previous SI could not be found.
When the SI cannot be found, the reconciliation process records all missing SI entries, resulting in an excessively large data set and causing an error when saving to the database.
As a result, the system fails to generate the EOD files.

Resolution:
-Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
-Informed SMthat no EOD files were generated for SVI Baguio TD: 02/13/2026. The root cause analysis, temporary and long-term solutions were also provided.
-Upon checking, POS 47 had no transactions from February 1 to February 12. However, on February 13, POS 047 was used and recorded a high volume of transactions.
-Note:POS #047 is included in the list of POS that have not been used for at least one month.-Asked Maam Chanda's approval to proceed with the necessary corrective actions.
-DMall R&D manually add a reconciliation record with the status set toFailed.
-AdvisedSM POS team to click the"ManualSuccess"in the Reconciliation page to generate theEOD files.
-Informed SM that the EOD files were already generated.
-Added this ticket to Problem 322.Resolved the ticket.
Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:

NO AUTOMATIC FLOAT WAS GENERATED FOR ALL OPENING CASHIERS AT POS 17,15,7 LAST FEB 14,2026

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:NO AUTOMATIC FLOAT WAS GENERATED FOR ALL OPENING CASHIERS
Root Cause Analysis:ISP downtime
POS can't connect to the ISP during cashier login because of ISP shutdown

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2.Based on the logs, the ISP experienced downtime from 15:31 PM to 10:05 AM on February 13-14, 2026.During this period, all POS terminals were unable to connect to the ISP at the time of cashier login. As a result, there were no automatic float/loan.3. Informed the store that this is a normal system behavior under such scenario.
4. Also advised them toensure that the POS terminals have a stable network connection during operation and that the ISP is up and running.
5.Resolved the ticket.

Adjust the settings and parameters on the printer setting until the left outmost part but still

解决摘要: Configuration Change

解决方案:
Define Issue:"Item Barcode Paper" tag printing issue

Root Cause Analysis:Support Group Action Issue
SM IT (Reenan Tabilin) changed the "Item Barcode Paper" template paper width size configuration from "91.5mm" to "75mm" on November 13, 2025 causing thelast barcode to be cut off when printing tags using the“Item Barcode Paper”template.


Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2.Found out thatthe issue was caused by a configuration change performed by SM IT (Reenan Tabilin) on November 13, 2025, wherein the paper width size for the "Item Barcode Paper" template was modified from 91.5mm to 75mm.3.Sent an approval request email to Maam Katt Cruz to correct the configurationin the Production environment forSMCo Tenant only.
4. R&D team fixed the configuration upon SM approval.

【Promotion id:26021221904000017 Mastercard Bank Promo 2026: Feb 15-March 15, 2026 ERROR on some POS】
问题: Promotion id:26021221904000017 Mastercard Bank Promo 2026: Feb 15-March 15, 2026 ERROR on some POS

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Apps - User Inquiry / Knowledge

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request For checking of error encounter to some pos regarding our on going mastercard bank promo. Please see attached file for the error encountered.
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue: Feb 21, 2026

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:Promotion id:26021221904000017 Mastercard Bank Promo 2026: Feb 15-March 15, 2026 ERROR on some POS
Root Cause Analysis:Inquiry / User Knowledge

Resolution:
Acknowledged the ticket.
Contacting the store to clarify their issue and provide more details.
Upon checking with our R&D team, item HARVESTERS-RICE SNANDOMENG_BAGO-25kg (Barcode 4809010955593) had a price override applied with the reason wrong shelf tag. Under the current system configuration, any item with a price override is excluded from promotion computation and its value is not counted toward the minimum spend requirement. Because the overridden item’s amount was excluded, the remaining transaction total fell below the required Php 5,000.00 minimum. Therefore, the transaction did not qualify for the promotion, and the freebie PF-TJ HDOG_JMBO_ORIG-500G (Barcode 4808887304176) was not granted.
We contacted the store and informed Ma’am Rose of SVI Dasmariñas, who confirmed that this ticket can now be resolved. 
We will now proceed in resolving this ticket.

解决方案:

Issue Description:Error While Scanning Using Print Request in PDA for E shelves 

Troubleshooting process:
1. In relation with ticket#6560227,this is regarding the“E‑Shelves Perfect Aisle” Project, in which stores use thePrint Requestapplication on the PDA to scan all articles and input the Bay, Layer, Facing, Height, Depth, and Sequence.
2. Objective:
3. To ensure 100% shelf availability and strengthen monitoring of articles by the assigned personnel—supporting both personnel accountability and shelf efficiency.
4. Please note that the“Qty” field in the application only accepts up to 10 numeric characters.
5. For more detailed information, you may coordinate directly with your Operations Trainers or OPC.
6. This isnot a transactional error, andno inventory adjustment is required.7. Resolved.

Advised the store to repost the order number to generate new GR in SAP.
Verified in DMall web that the order number has been reposted.
Will now proceed in resolving this ticket.

【81 Hybrid Store Sales Intergration file  not loaded  to DMALL dated:02-25-2026】
问题: 81 Hybrid Store Sales Intergration file  not loaded  to DMALL dated:02-25-2026

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Integration Failure

问题描述: 81 Hybrid Store Sales Integration file not loaded to DMALL dated:02-25-2026

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue: Hybrid Stores Sales Data Integration Issue (atleast 100 stores)

Root Cause Analysis:DMall system bug.
When the number of Hybrid stores (using DMall Inventory only) exceeds 100, a system interface limitation is triggered, resulting in errors that prevent sales files from being loaded from the SM SFTP to the DMall system.

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated with R&D.
2.Informed SM teamthat the issue was caused by DMall system bug. When the number of Hybrid stores (using DMall Inventory only) exceeds 100, a system interface limitation is triggered, resulting in errors that prevent sales files from being loaded from the SM SFTP to the DMall system.
3. Added toProblem No. 329 and DMall asked SM approval to deploy an emergency release to fix the issue in the UAT and PROD environment since there's no available temporary solution.
4.Long-Term Solution:The system interface will be enhanced to process requests in batches, ensuring that each interface call remains below the 100-store limit.
5.The fix was successfully validated in the UAT environment and subsequently deployed to Production upon SM’s approval (Release Scope: 202602_9_PRODFIX_INV).6.Ma’am Lea from the SM POS Support and Dev team confirmed that all 83 pending sales files for Transaction Date (TD) February 25, 2026, as well as all sales files from 103 stores for TD February 26, 2026, were successfully and automatically loaded into the DMall system.Resolved the ticket.

Release Notes/Version:-
Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

team.

above.

解决摘要: Temporary / Quick Solution (Workaround)

解决方案:
Define Issue:No generated EOD files for SMCo Angono 2 TD: 2/26/2026

Root Cause Analysis:Expired SMAC was used during testing before Go-Live

Resolution:

2.Informed Maam Chanda that the issue was caused by the expired SMAC used during testing before Go-Live. The after-sales transaction9560306021260226013522001 remains in "Refund in Process" status which resulted to non-generation of EOD files.
3. Asked SM approval to fix the affected transaction.
4.R&D team updated the refund transaction status from "Refund in process" to "Refund Successful" and reran the EOD files.
5.SM Apps Support confirmed thatthe EOD files are now complete and available in their respective SFTP folders.Resolved the ticket.

【SOME ARTICLES HAD NO DISPLAY OF PRICE PER UOM ON SHELFTAG】
问题: SOME ARTICLES HAD NO DISPLAY OF PRICE PER UOM ON SHELFTAG

根因分类: Inquiry / User Knowledge

具体根因: Investigation Ongoing

问题描述: Ticket Creation Template
Description of your issue or request
WHILE PRINTING SHELFTAG WE NOTICE SOME ARTICLES HAD NO DISPLAY OF PRICE PER UOM AS SEEN ON THE ATTACHMENTS.
Affected Application:
SHELF LABEL
Affected Asset No.

S

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Please be informed that for any articles with grammage set to a divisor of 1, regardless of UOM (e.g., liter or kg), the grammage per UOM will not appear on the shelf tag when printed in TPS. Upon checking in SAP, all these articles do not have a net content value maintained. This issue is similar to ticket #6576471, please refer to it for reference.

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
This is regarding the “E‑Shelves Perfect Aisle” Project, in which stores use the Print Request application on the PDA to scan all articles and input the Bay, Layer, Facing, Height, Depth, and Sequence.
Objective:
To ensure 100% shelf availability and strengthen monitoring of articles
 by the assigned personnel—supporting both personnel accountability and 
shelf efficiency.
Please note that the “Qty” field in the application only accepts up to 10 numeric characters.
For more detailed information, you may coordinate directly with your Operations Trainers or OPC.
This is not a transactional error, and no inventory adjustment is required.

I
 have already contacted you Sir Archie via phone call and through viber,
 and as an advise from IT Functional Sir Elvis, kindly concern this to 
Sir Dennis (or other OPC Trainors for more assistance, this might be 
procedural error). We will proceed with resolving this ticket. Should 
you have any questions or additional comments, kindly provide them 
within five (5) days. Otherwise, the ticket will be automatically closed. You may refer to this tickets for more information. #6560227and #6548682.

Thank you.
Alyssa

-Net Discount=₱12.55
-Net Transaction Discount forReceipt No.559201034260304130513020050is₱12.55.

【No automatic loan slip】
问题: No automatic loan slip

根因分类: Equipment Failure

具体根因: Hardware - ISP Restart / Shutdown

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue:During the cashiers Log in at the counters, POS did not generate automatic loan slips in all terminals, 3 cashiers have already logged in without receiving automatic l

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define Issue:No automatic loan slip 
Root Cause Analysis:ISP downtime
POS can't connect to the ISP during cashier login because of ISP shutdown

Resolution:
1. Acknowledged the ticket.
2.Based on the logs, the ISP experienced downtime from 8:51 AM to 9:19 AM on March 5, 2026, as shown in the screenshot below.
During this period, all POS terminals were unable to connect to the ISP at the time of cashier login. As a result, there were no automatic float/loan.​3. Informed the store that this is a normal system behavior under such scenario.
4. Also advised them toensure that the POS terminals have a stable network connection during operation and that the ISP is up and running.
5.Resolved the ticket.

【Request for Last SI on POS 8 & 9 on BIR Report】
问题: Request for Last SI on POS 8 & 9 on BIR Report

根因分类: Defect from Dmall

具体根因: Apps - Application Issue

问题描述: Type: Incident / Request
Response Level:Level A / B / C / D
Details of Issue: No last SI generated on POS 8 & 9 on BIR Report

解决摘要: Log to Problem

解决方案:
Define Issue:Request for Last SI on POS 8 & 9 on BIR Report​
Root Cause Analysis: Defect from DMall

Resolution:
- Acknowledged the ticket.
- Coordinate with out R&D.
-. According to our R&D, for POS#008 & POS#009 the last transaction was in November 2025, and there were no transactions after that for a long time.In the daily Term Z data reported to BIR, since there were no transactions, the Beg SI and End SI remained empty. On the Big Data report side, there is a compensation logic: if the SI is empty, the system will retrieve the most recent record that has an SI and use it to fill in the missing value. However, this logic has a time limit of 2 months.
-Since this POS had no transactions for more than 2 months, the system could not retrieve a previous SI. Only when a recent transaction occurred did the SI appear again, that means there were no transaction records from 2025.11.04 to 2026.03.05.
-Upon checking, for POS#008 & POS#009 BIR sales report is already exist.
-Note:
If the POS has no transactions and the SI is empty, the system will check the last transaction record to get the SI. It can only look back up to 60 days. If there is no transaction within 60 days, the system will show “-”. Once the POS has a new transaction, the SI will show normally again.
-Basic Rule:
For dates without transaction data, the system will display the SI from the most recent date that had a transaction.
-Long-term solution:
When the POS client reports summary data to BIR via Term Z, if there are no transactions for the day, it will use the Term Z receipt fallback logic to send the Beg SI and End SI from the receipt.
-The ticket is resolved.

Release Notes/Version:-Remarks/Recommendation:-
Data Collection/References:

Response Level:Level A / B / C / D

Good Day!

I would like to report a scenario encountered during annual stocktake. Accounting supervisor approach us that bay barcode 02171 had problem during editin

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
Define
Issue:Annual Stocktake: System error ecounter
Root
Cause Analysis:Defect from DMall

Resolution:
Acknowledged the ticket and coordinated the issue to our R&D.
Based on our investigation, before the initial stock take for Bay Barcode 02171 was submitted by user OPS Angelica De Guzman, article 20580754 was deleted on 03/08/2026 at 8:49 AM. However, another user had already created a recount form at 8:50 AM with the outdated list that still included article 20580754. Since the article had already been deleted from the initial stock take, it resulted in a null value for the article, which caused the abnormal scenario.For short-term solution, DMall manually corrected the value of article 20580754 and since the store already created a new bay barcode(02263) for the affected article, they need to make a new recount to zero out bay barcode 02171.
With the approval from Ma'am Katt Cruz, DMall proceed in the fix and SSM OPC helped with the recount and spotcheck to align the inventory.
SSM OPC confirmed that issue has been fixed and inventory is aligned.

【REQUEST FOR REVERSAL OF STDR DUE TO PROCESS ON WRONG SLOC LOCATION CODE】
问题: REQUEST FOR REVERSAL OF STDR DUE TO PROCESS ON WRONG SLOC LOCATION CODE

根因分类: User Error

具体根因: Apps - User Procedural Problem

问题描述: Type:SETTLEMENT
Response Level:Level A
Details of Issue: REQUEST FOR REVERSAL OF STDR DUE TO PROCESS ON WRONG SLOC LOCATION CODE

CORRECT LOCATION CODE: 0010
ISSUING SITE : 3903 STO TOMAS
RECIEVING SITE : 2342 TANAUAN

STO
#20358975

解决摘要: Normal Application Fix

解决方案:
​Root Cause:User Error/REQUEST FOR REVERSAL OF STDR DUE TO PROCESS ON WRONG SLOC LOCATION CODEProblem 184.

Issue Description:REQUEST FOR REVERSAL OF STDR DUE TO PROCESS ON WRONG SLOC LOCATION CODE


Troubleshooting process:
1.Acknowledge the ticket.
2.Upon checking,this issue has been encountered in our past tickets listed in our problem management asproblem183. STO2035897598was not serve.



3. The system does not support the "Not Served" status when the store does not receive all items listed under the Document Number (DN) or Seal Number. This scenario had not been encountered previously, as there was no prior instance where the issuing site failed to deliver all items to the store.
Example:For a DN containing 10 items, if 2 items are unserved, the system can still proceed—posting the remaining 8 items and generating a GR number. However, in the case of DN0074945190, which contains only 2 articles that was not delivered to the store, the system is unable to proceed. As a result, the status remains stuck at "Posting."
Short Term Solution:
DMall will manually trigger the creation of STDR.
DMall will tag the order number to "No Need.
Long-term Solution:We have logged this issue under Problem No.183.

4. Good day,Our R&D Team already tag the order #IB12342202603120001to no need and already have an STDR.
Please refer to the image below.
6


5. Resolved.
